At this time, the corridor and outdoor temperatures were lower than indoors. I went out for a walk and thought that the temperature would always drop when I came back at night. As a result, the room was still very hot when I came back. The air conditioner didn't work at all. It blew out hot air. The indoor temperature was nearly 30 degrees. After repeated requests, the hotel turned over an air conditioner fan in the warehouse at more than 10 o'clock in the evening, but the sound was very loud and the cooling effect was not good at all. It was the kind of thing that would kill you if you didn't turn it on, and it would kill you if you turned it on. I didn't sleep well all night.
Hygiene: The hotel hygiene is average. Because it is relatively old, the accumulated water stains on the sink can't be wiped clean, and the carpet is not cleaned.
Service: The service is average. The hotel is too inefficient in dealing with the air conditioning problem. The breakfast is very average and far from worth looking forward to. Moreover, when the breakfast time is about to end but not over, when there are guests eating, the lights in the restaurant are turned off. . .
To sum up, it doesn't have the environment and service that Hilton should have, and is no different from an old-fashioned business hotel. . . .
